Important! In the Russian Federation, a mobile boarding pass is not accepted as a substitute for a normal (printed) boarding pass. In Russia, you should have your mobile boarding pass printed at the airport, either using the special terminals or with the help of S7 staff at a check-in counter, before you go through security control.

How do I use the mobile boarding pass?

Arrive at the airport well in advance – one and a half to two hours before the flight departure. You’ll need some time to check-in your luggage and go through all the airport formalities. Check-in usually closes 40 minutes before the scheduled departure, and boarding usually 25 minutes before departure.

The S7 app also allows you to:
• Check in
